Riddle: you burry the survivers in heaven  Fork: for 36/38 orange lowwers Drivetrain: trp drivetrain
Okay lets talk tyre inserts. Put the tyre on without the insert first, inflate it and get it seated. Make sure it holds pressure without sealant. Then let the air out and open one side of the tyre so you can put the insert in. Once you have the insert inside the tyre start putting the tyre back on from the opposite side of the valve. The key is to get the tyre into the middle of the rim and underneath the insert. I've found that pressing on the tyre with something that has a round end works perfectly. Then once you get to the bit where you can't get further without the other side of the tyre starting to come out take some straps or zip ties and make sure you get one side 'locked'. Add some lubricant to the edge of the tyre (I use a silicone stick, the kind that you rub on your car door seals during winter) and then wiggle the rest of the tyre in. If you're using metal levers or breaking plastic ones then you're doing something wrong. Also do not add sealant before you've tested that the tyre holds air.
